%   The Italian corpus used in Gervain and Guevara (under review).
%   The corpus contains the child-directed adult utterances of four Italian subcorpora (Antelmi corpus, Calambrone corpus, Rome corpus, Tonelli corpus) of the CHILDES database. The corpus was processed for the purposes of the study. The processing is described in detail in Gervain and Guevara (under review).
%   Note that the corpus was phonotypically transcribed, so the characters indicate phonemes, i.e. pronunciation, not actual graphemes.
%   1 = unvoiced post alveolar affricate, as in ciao 'hello' (like English ch in church)
%   2 = voiced alveolar affricate, as in pizza 'pizza' (like English ds in Leeds)
%   3 = voiced postalveolar affricate, as in giorno 'day' (like English j in jungle) 
%   4 = palatal lateral approximant, as in gli 'the' (masc. plural)
%   5 = palatal nasal, as in agnello 'lamb' (similar to the palatal prnunciation of n in new)
%   6 = voiceless alveolar fricative, as in serio 'serious' (like English s in see)
%   9 = voiced velar nasal, as in anche 'also' (like English ng in sing)


%   Boundary notation:
%   UB = utterance boundary
%   WB = word boundary
%   WI = word innternal (i.e. no boundary)

%   Publications using this corpus should cite:
Gervain, Judit & Guevara Erra, Ramon. (under review). "The Statistical Signature of Morphosyntax: A Study of Hungarian and Italian Infant-Directed Speech".
